from geopy.geocoders import Nominatim
from geopy.extra.rate_limiter import RateLimiter
import pandas as pd
import os
# # Check if the file exists
# if os.path.exists('./assets/locations.csv'):
#     # Load the DataFrame from the CSV file
#     df_locations = pd.read_csv('./assets/locations.csv')
# else:
#     # Create a new DataFrame with the specified columns
#     df_locations = pd.DataFrame(columns=['id', 'address', 'latitude', 'longitude'])
#     df_locations.to_csv('./assets/locations.csv', index=False)
df = pd.read_csv('./assets/data.csv')
# Create a geolocator object
geolocator = Nominatim(user_agent="baqapp")

# Rate limiter to avoid hitting API limits
geocode = RateLimiter(geolocator.geocode, min_delay_seconds=1)
def get_lat_lon(address, lat_col, lon_col):
    try:
        if pd.isnull(lat_col) and pd.isnull(lon_col):
            location = geocode(address + ", Barranquilla, Colombia")
            if location:
                return location.latitude, location.longitude, True
            else:
                return None, None, False
        else:
            return lat_col, lon_col, True
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"Error: {e}")
        return None, None, False
    
# Initialize a counter
iteration_count = 0
start_at = 16050
max_iteration = 20000

df = pd.read_csv('./assets/data.csv')

# Apply the function to the DataFrame, saving every 10 iterations
for index, row in df.iterrows():
    if (index < start_at): continue

    lat, lon, success = get_lat_lon(row['address'], row['latitude'], row['longitude'])

    if (success): print(f"fount at {index} - {row['address']}")

    df.loc[index, ['latitude', 'longitude']] = lat, lon
    iteration_count += 1

    # Save the DataFrame to CSV every 10 iterations
    if iteration_count % 10 == 0:
        df.to_csv('./assets/data.csv', index=False)
        print(f"Checkpoint saved at index {index} iteration {iteration_count}")

    if(iteration_count >= max_iteration):
      break

# Save the final DataFrame
df.to_csv('./assets/data.csv', index=False)
